## Instruction

My personal information is stored in Memory. The workspace contains my course schedule and a master exam table (in Excel format). The courses I need to take this semester are in list.txt.
Please help me choose the right courses. I can only take one of each course. I have club activities in the evening, so I'll only take daytime courses. Also, my favorite teacher is Yulian(郁莲). if she teaches any required courses, please make sure to take her.
Based on my personal information, please first help me find the right specific courses. Then, help me find the exams I need to take this semester. Save the exam information in the workspace in a file named exam_schedule.jsonl. The format should refer to `format.md`.
All information must match the Excel file. If a course is not required this semester(Course exemption), omit it. Finally, sort the objects in the JSONL file by exam time.

## Initial State

### Local Workspace

There are more than 500 files in the workspace.

```python 
# Let me create a more systematic approach to extract exam information
# I'll read the Excel file and extract the relevant data

import json

# Load the Excel data from the overlong output file
with open('/workspace/dumps/workspace/.overlong_tool_outputs/jT5qeCTAV7Ni6dAWGXzeYo.json', 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
    excel_data = json.load(f)

# Parse the cells data
cells_data = excel_data['cells']

# Create a structured representation of the Excel data
rows = {}
for cell in cells_data:
    row_num = cell['row']
    col_num = cell['column']
    value = cell['value']
    
    if row_num not in rows:
        rows[row_num] = {}
    rows[row_num][col_num] = value

# Extract header row to understand column structure
headers = rows[1]
print("Excel headers:")
for col, header in headers.items():
    print(f"Column {col}: {header}")

print("\n" + "="*50)

# My target course codes
target_courses = {
    "01711100": "算法分析与设计",
    "61410004": "新时代中国特色社会主义理论与实践", 
    "01710101": "自然辩证法概论",
    "01711870": "综合实践",
    "01710110": "英语"
}

# Find matching exams
matching_exams = []

for row_num, row_data in rows.items():
    if row_num == 1:  # Skip header
        continue
        
    course_code = row_data.get(1, "")  # Column 1 is course code
    course_name = row_data.get(2, "")  # Column 2 is course name
    
    # Check if this row matches any of my target courses
    for target_code, target_name in target_courses.items():
        if target_code in str(course_code):
            exam_info = {
                "course_code": course_code,
                "course_name": course_name,
                "target_object": row_data.get(3, ""),  # Column 3
                "exam_type": row_data.get(4, ""),      # Column 4
                "time_period": row_data.get(5, ""),    # Column 5
                "exam_date": row_data.get(6, ""),      # Column 6
                "exam_time": row_data.get(7, ""),      # Column 7
                "exam_room": row_data.get(8, ""),      # Column 8
                "num_students": row_data.get(9, ""),   # Column 9
                "notes": row_data.get(10, ""),         # Column 10
                "contact_person": row_data.get(11, "") # Column 11
            }
            matching_exams.append(exam_info)
            print(f"Found exam for {target_name}:")
            print(f"  Course Code: {exam_info['course_code']}")
            print(f"  Course Name: {exam_info['course_name']}")
            print(f"  Target Object: {exam_info['target_object']}")
            print(f"  Exam Type: {exam_info['exam_type']}")
            print(f"  Exam Date: {exam_info['exam_date']}")
            print(f"  Exam Time: {exam_info['exam_time']}")
            print(f"  Exam Room: {exam_info['exam_room']}")
            print(f"  Contact: {exam_info['contact_person']}")
            print()

print(f"Total matching exams found: {len(matching_exams)}")
```

```python 
# Let me extract the exam information from the Excel data
import json
from datetime import datetime

# Parse the Excel data
with open('/workspace/dumps/workspace/.overlong_tool_outputs/TETNtPRiztM6edncE8rmCi.json', 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
    excel_data = json.load(f)

cells_data = excel_data['cells']

# Create a structured representation
rows = {}
for cell in cells_data:
    row_num = cell['row']
    col_num = cell['column']
    value = cell['value']
    
    if row_num not in rows:
        rows[row_num] = {}
    rows[row_num][col_num] = value

# My student ID to check if I'm in the target range
my_student_id = "2401210477"

# Target courses and their information
target_courses = {
    "61410004": {"name": "新时代中国特色社会主义理论与实践", "teacher": "研究生院"},
    "01710101": {"name": "自然辩证法概论（1班）", "teacher": "朱效民"},
    "01711870": {"name": "综合实践（3班）-集成电路与智能系统系", "teacher": "导师小组"},
    "01710110": {"name": "英语（2班-4班）", "teacher": "李博婷/高志军"},
    "01711100": {"name": "算法分析与设计-01班", "teacher": "郁莲"}
}

matching_exams = []

# Check each row for matching courses
for row_num, row_data in rows.items():
    if row_num == 1:  # Skip header
        continue
        
    course_code = str(row_data.get(1, "")).replace(",", "").strip()
    course_name = str(row_data.get(2, "")).strip()
    target_object = str(row_data.get(3, "")).strip()
    exam_type = str(row_data.get(4, "")).strip()
    time_period = str(row_data.get(5, "")).strip()
    exam_date = str(row_data.get(6, "")).strip()
    exam_time = str(row_data.get(7, "")).strip()
    exam_room = str(row_data.get(8, "")).strip()
    num_students = str(row_data.get(9, "")).strip()
    notes = str(row_data.get(10, "")).strip()
    contact_person = str(row_data.get(11, "")).strip()
    
    # Check if this matches any of my target courses
    for target_code, target_info in target_courses.items():
        if target_code in course_code:
            # Check if this is for Electronic Information students
            if "电子信息" in target_object:
                # Check if my student ID is in the range (if specified)
                if notes and "-" in notes:
                    # Check student ID range
                    try:
                        start_id, end_id = notes.split("-")
                        if start_id <= my_student_id <= end_id:
                            in_range = True
                        else:
                            in_range = False
                    except:
                        in_range = True  # If can't parse, assume it's valid
                else:
                    in_range = True
                
                if in_range:
                    exam_info = {
                        "course_code": course_code,
                        "course_name": course_name,
                        "target_object": target_object,
                        "exam_type": exam_type,
                        "time_period": time_period,
                        "exam_date": exam_date,
                        "exam_time": exam_time,
                        "exam_room": exam_room,
                        "num_students": num_students,
                        "notes": notes,
                        "contact_person": contact_person,
                        "target_name": target_info["name"],
                        "expected_teacher": target_info["teacher"]
                    }
                    matching_exams.append(exam_info)
                    print(f"✓ Found exam for {target_info['name']}:")
                    print(f"  Course Code: {course_code}")
                    print(f"  Course Name: {course_name}")
                    print(f"  Exam Type: {exam_type}")
                    print(f"  Exam Date: {exam_date}")
                    print(f"  Exam Time: {exam_time}")
                    print(f"  Exam Room: {exam_room}")
                    print(f"  Contact: {contact_person}")
                    if notes:
                        print(f"  Student Range: {notes}")
                    print()

print(f"Total matching exams found: {len(matching_exams)}")

# Check which courses are missing
found_codes = [exam["course_code"] for exam in matching_exams]
missing_courses = []
for code, info in target_courses.items():
    if not any(code in found_code for found_code in found_codes):
        missing_courses.append(f"{code}: {info['name']}")

if missing_courses:
    print(f"\nMissing courses (may not have formal exams):")
    for course in missing_courses:
        print(f"  - {course}")
```

```python 
# Create the final exam schedule based on the Excel data
import json
from datetime import datetime

# My selected courses and their corresponding exams
# Based on the Excel data and my requirements

my_student_id = "2401210477"

# Final exam list based on Excel data and my course selections
exams = [
    {
        "courseName": "新时代中国特色社会主义理论与实践",
        "teacher": "研究生院",
        "examAdministrator": "赵泽宇",
        "examDate": "2024.11.25（一）",
        "examTime": "13:00-15:00",
        "examRoom": "3303",
        "examType": "闭卷"
    },
    {
        "courseName": "自然辩证法概论（1班）",
        "teacher": "朱效民",
        "examAdministrator": "赵泽宇", 
        "examDate": "2024.11.25（一）",
        "examTime": "10:00-12:00",
        "examRoom": "3310",
        "examType": "闭卷"
    },
    {
        "courseName": "英语（2班-3班）",
        "teacher": "李博婷",
        "examAdministrator": "赵泽宇",
        "examDate": "2024.12.07（六）", 
        "examTime": "9:00-11:00",
        "examRoom": "3302",
        "examType": "闭卷"
    },
    {
        "courseName": "综合实践（1班）-软件工程与数据技术系",
        "teacher": "导师小组",
        "examAdministrator": "许博蕊",
        "examDate": "2025.01.02（一）",
        "examTime": "08:00-09:00", 
        "examRoom": "线上",
        "examType": "开卷"
    },
    {
        "courseName": "算法分析与设计-01、02班",
        "teacher": "郁莲",
        "examAdministrator": "许博蕊",
        "examDate": "2025.01.11（六）",
        "examTime": "9:00-11:00",
        "examRoom": "3302",  # My student ID 2401210477 is in range 2401210399-2401210800, so room 3302
        "examType": "闭卷"
    }
]

# Function to convert date to sortable format
def get_sort_key(exam):
    date_str = exam["examDate"]
    # Extract date part and convert to sortable format
    if "2024.11.25" in date_str:
        return "2024-11-25" + exam["examTime"]
    elif "2024.12.07" in date_str:
        return "2024-12-07" + exam["examTime"] 
    elif "2025.01.02" in date_str:
        return "2025-01-02" + exam["examTime"]
    elif "2025.01.11" in date_str:
        return "2025-01-11" + exam["examTime"]
    return date_str

# Sort exams by date and time
exams_sorted = sorted(exams, key=get_sort_key)

print("Final exam schedule (sorted by date and time):")
for i, exam in enumerate(exams_sorted, 1):
    print(f"{i}. {exam['courseName']}")
    print(f"   Teacher: {exam['teacher']}")
    print(f"   Date: {exam['examDate']}")
    print(f"   Time: {exam['examTime']}")
    print(f"   Room: {exam['examRoom']}")
    print(f"   Type: {exam['examType']}")
    print(f"   Administrator: {exam['examAdministrator']}")
    print()

# Save to JSONL file
jsonl_content = ""
for exam in exams_sorted:
    jsonl_content += json.dumps(exam, ensure_ascii=False) + "\n"

print("JSONL content to be saved:")
print(jsonl_content)
```
